{\bfseries 值\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ ((idx)\ =\ 0,\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}})\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a0ea8514c92f39fd93ddcbe93a7f466e5}{yyjson\_arr\_size}}(arr),\ \(\backslash\)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ (idx)\ <\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}});\ (idx)++,\ (val)\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a5f0626a64dccd0288d42b1a52bca64ec}{unsafe\_yyjson\_get\_next}}(val))}

\end{DoxyCode}
Macro for iterating over an array. It works like iterator, but with a more intuitive API.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ idx,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\_val}}\ *val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a60fd8094ee3eff6e7b629471f50aa139}{yyjson\_arr\_foreach}}(arr,\ idx,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}},\ val)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ your\_func(idx,\ val);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

compiler version (MSVC) \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a23a525f4192a237730aedfad55798fdb}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_arr\_foreach@{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_foreach}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_foreach}{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_foreach}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a23a525f4192a237730aedfad55798fdb} 
\#define yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+arr\+\_\+foreach(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{arr}{, }\item[{}]{idx}{, }\item[{}]{\mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}}}{, }\item[{}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries 值\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ ((idx)\ =\ 0,\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}})\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a847bb374b9c7fa6fff34088d23d87dad}{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_size}}(arr),\ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ (val)\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a9ff667f95ec6e6e264509e1681c74357}{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_get\_first}}(arr);\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ (idx)\ <\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}});\ (idx)++,\ (val)\ =\ (val)-\/>\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val_a172090776a18e45190c933fb3294c07c}{next}})}

\end{DoxyCode}
Macro for iterating over an array. It works like iterator, but with a more intuitive API.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
You should not modify the array while iterating over it.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ idx,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\_mut\_val}}\ *val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a23a525f4192a237730aedfad55798fdb}{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_foreach}}(arr,\ idx,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{datatypes_8h_affe776513b24d84b39af8ab0930fef7f}{max}},\ val)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ your\_func(idx,\ val);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\end{DoxyCode}
Macro for iterating over an object. It works like iterator, but with a more intuitive API.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
You should not modify the object while iterating over it.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aca9bf31696b79fb45b57dd0e016b272d} 
typedef struct yyjson\+\_\+doc yyjson\+\_\+doc}

An immutable document for reading JSON. This document holds memory for all its JSON values and strings. When it is no longer used, the user should call {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}} to free its memory. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a8742a526ad3fb54bcf7eea9bf557f15b}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_arr\_iter@{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_iter}}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\end{DoxyParagraph}

typedef struct yyjson\+\_\+ptr\+\_\+ctx yyjson\+\_\+ptr\+\_\+ctx}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} context for JSON pointer operation.

This struct stores the context of JSON Pointer operation result. The struct can be used with three helper functions\+: {\ttfamily ctx\+\_\+append()}, {\ttfamily ctx\+\_\+replace()}, and {\ttfamily ctx\+\_\+remove()}, which perform the corresponding operations on the container without re-\/parsing the JSON Pointer.

For example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ doc\ before:\ \{"{}a"{}:[0,1,null]\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ ptr:\ "{}/a/2"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{val\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a6031b6b35b06127f3fa2278be67c29ea}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_ptr\_getx}}(doc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a26c622783fa717b24fe0bbd3e060f74a}{ptr}},\ strlen(\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a26c622783fa717b24fe0bbd3e060f74a}{ptr}}),\ \&ctx,\ \&err);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a81cc3185457d7fd86f3818319d7efe18}{yyjson\_is\_null}}(val))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a92d8ec53e4cf8426288d86868dc89e09}{yyjson\_ptr\_ctx\_remove}}(\&ctx);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ doc\ after:\ \{"{}a"{}:[0,1]\}}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aaa9b7978e7b40e6d5d8d1cb3da0568d6}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free()}{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_free()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aaa9b7978e7b40e6d5d8d1cb3da0568d6} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+free (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Free a dynamic allocator which is created by {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a6a90ae91b82c2e8d6665a28a691eee18}{yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+new()}}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em alc} & The dynamic allocator to be destroyed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a6a90ae91b82c2e8d6665a28a691eee18}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new@{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new()}{yyjson\_alc\_dyn\_new()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a6a90ae91b82c2e8d6665a28a691eee18} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+new (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} dynamic allocator.

This allocator has a similar usage to the pool allocator above. However, when there is not enough memory, this allocator will dynamically request more memory using libc\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily malloc} function, and frees it all at once when it is destroyed.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new dynamic allocator, or NULL if memory allocation failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The returned value should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_aaa9b7978e7b40e6d5d8d1cb3da0568d6}{yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+dyn\+\_\+free()}}.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This Allocator is not thread-\/safe. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 9
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a6068c4293a2b35493b18421b9afbd3d5}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init@{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}}
\index{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init@{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init()}{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a6068c4293a2b35493b18421b9afbd3d5} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+alc\+\_\+pool\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pool allocator uses fixed length pre-\/allocated memory.

This allocator may be used to avoid malloc/realloc calls. The pre-\/allocated memory should be held by the caller. The maximum amount of memory required to read a JSON can be calculated using the {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ae511cac592355c2f60f170402b9d8dbf}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+max\+\_\+memory\+\_\+usage()}} function, but the amount of memory required to write a JSON cannot be directly calculated.

This is not a general-\/purpose allocator. It is designed to handle a single JSON data at a time. If it is used for overly complex memory tasks, such as parsing multiple JSON documents using the same allocator but releasing only a few of them, it may cause memory fragmentation, resulting in performance degradation and memory waste.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em alc} & The allocator to be initialized. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return false. If {\ttfamily buf} or {\ttfamily size} is invalid, this will be set to an empty allocator. \\
\hline
{\em buf} & The buffer memory for this allocator. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
{\em size} & The size of {\ttfamily buf}, in bytes. If this parameter is less than 8 words (32/64 bytes on 32/64-\/bit OS), the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if the {\ttfamily alc} has been successfully initialized.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ parse\ JSON\ with\ stack\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ buf[1024];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\_alc}}\ alc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a6068c4293a2b35493b18421b9afbd3d5}{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}}(\&alc,\ buf,\ 1024);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ *\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenlohmann_a8ba8c5483f73a36e716558571ff97d57}{json}}\ =\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\{\(\backslash\)"{}name\(\backslash\)"{}:\(\backslash\)"{}Helvetica\(\backslash\)"{},\(\backslash\)"{}size\(\backslash\)"{}:16\}"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\_doc}}\ *doc\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}{yyjson\_read\_opts}}(json,\ strlen(json),\ 0,\ \&alc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ memory\ of\ \`{}doc`\ is\ on\ the\ stack}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This Allocator is not thread-\/safe. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ac709738fbf9da708c28992c40746fcbf}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_arr\_get@{yyjson\_arr\_get}}
\index{yyjson\_arr\_get@{yyjson\_arr\_get}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_arr\_get()}{yyjson\_arr\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ac709738fbf9da708c28992c40746fcbf} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+arr\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{arr}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{idx}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the element at the specified position in this array. Returns NULL if array is NULL/empty or the index is out of bounds. \begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if array is not flat. For example\+: {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,\{\},3\mbox{]}} is flat, {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},3\mbox{]}} is not flat. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Returns the first element of this array. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily arr} is NULL/empty or type is not array. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a15bbce96107aa455670ebe9aab98964d}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_arr\_get\_last@{yyjson\_arr\_get\_last}}
\index{yyjson\_arr\_get\_last@{yyjson\_arr\_get\_last}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_arr\_get\_last()}{yyjson\_arr\_get\_last()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a15bbce96107aa455670ebe9aab98964d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+arr\+\_\+get\+\_\+last (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{arr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the last element of this array. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily arr} is NULL/empty or type is not array. \begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if array is not flat. For example\+: {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,\{\},3\mbox{]}} is flat, {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},3\mbox{]}} is not flat. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a95aebc83fff9793f7701a6e37df5e03f} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+arr\+\_\+iter\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{arr}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__arr__iter}{yyjson\+\_\+arr\+\_\+iter}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iter}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Initialize an iterator for this array.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em arr} & The array to be iterated over. If this parameter is NULL or not an array, {\ttfamily iter} will be set to empty. \\
\hline
{\em iter} & The iterator to be initialized. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if the {\ttfamily iter} has been successfully initialized.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The iterator does not need to be destroyed. 
\end{DoxyNote}

This function will do nothing if the {\ttfamily doc} is NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a33580e2537c25685fd1209951dcbc967}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_doc\_get\_read\_size@{yyjson\_doc\_get\_read\_size}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a083356ecb65e45453033285f3d836de9} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+mut\+\_\+copy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies and returns a new mutable document from input, returns NULL on error. This makes a {\ttfamily deep-\/copy} on the immutable document. If allocator is NULL, the default allocator will be used. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily imut\+\_\+doc} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily mut\+\_\+doc}. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a9a9b30d275e211df9b84b91f4b95907a}

Get value by a JSON Pointer. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_equals()}{yyjson\_equals()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_adabd9eb44fac843109d6bc79f12ff6ff} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+equals (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{lhs}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{rhs}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns whether two JSON values are equal (deep compare). Returns false if input is NULL. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
the result may be inaccurate if object has duplicate keys. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+is\+\_\+uint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns whether the JSON value is unsigned integer (\doxylink{eabase_8h_aaa5d1cd013383c889537491c3cfd9aad}{uint64\+\_\+t}). Returns false if {\ttfamily val} is NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ac742b11ff26fb9af6362ffd2f3f21061}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_locate\_pos@{yyjson\_locate\_pos}}
\index{yyjson\_locate\_pos@{yyjson\_locate\_pos}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_locate\_pos()}{yyjson\_locate\_pos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ac742b11ff26fb9af6362ffd2f3f21061} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+locate\+\_\+pos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{str}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{pos}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{line}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{col}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{chr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Locate the line and column number for a byte position in a string. This can be used to get better description for error position.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em str} & The input string. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The byte length of the input string. \\
\hline
{\em pos} & The byte position within the input string. \\
\hline
{\em line} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the line number, starting from 1. \\
\hline
{\em col} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the column number, starting from 1. \\
\hline
{\em chr} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive the character index, starting from 0. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true on success, false if {\ttfamily str} is NULL or {\ttfamily pos} is out of bounds. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Line/column/character are calculated based on Unicode characters for compatibility with text editors. For multi-\/byte UTF-\/8 characters, the returned value may not directly correspond to the byte position. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a9026faa4e022392c28e8f9afa553362f}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_merge\_patch@{yyjson\_merge\_patch}}
\index{yyjson\_merge\_patch@{yyjson\_merge\_patch}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_merge\_patch()}{yyjson\_merge\_patch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a9026faa4e022392c28e8f9afa553362f} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+merge\+\_\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{orig}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{patch}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a merge-\/patched JSON value (RFC 7386). The memory of the returned value is allocated by the {\ttfamily doc}. Returns NULL if the patch could not be applied.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_af7da1562cde867338bc69395c2aeb0ad} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+arr\+\_\+with\+\_\+str (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{vals}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a new mutable array with the given strings, these strings will not be copied.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} mutable document, used for memory allocation only. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em vals} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} C array of UTF-\/8 null-\/terminator strings. If this array contains NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em count} & The number of values in {\ttfamily vals}. If this value is 0, an empty array will return. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The new array. NULL if input is invalid or memory allocation failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The input strings are not copied, you should keep these strings unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. If these strings will be modified, you should use {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a90c3e1c55dcf04a7879abed9a57cb278}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+arr\+\_\+with\+\_\+strcpy()}} instead.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\end{DoxyCode}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a419008c4a6f2dc4221211b0d7770109a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+arr\+\_\+with\+\_\+strn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{vals}{, }\item[{const size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{lens}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a new mutable array with the given strings and string lengths, these strings will not be copied.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} mutable document, used for memory allocation only. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em vals} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} C array of UTF-\/8 strings, null-\/terminator is not required. If this array contains NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em lens} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} C array of string lengths, in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em count} & The number of strings in {\ttfamily vals}. If this value is 0, an empty array will return. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The new array. NULL if input is invalid or memory allocation failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The input strings are not copied, you should keep these strings unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. If these strings will be modified, you should use {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ad8c68a8cec010d2d5f8942eb1136afde}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+arr\+\_\+with\+\_\+strncpy()}} instead.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ *vals[3]\ =\ \{\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}a"{}},\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bb"{}},\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}c"{}}\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ lens[3]\ =\ \{\ 1,\ 2,\ 1\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\_mut\_val}}\ *arr\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a419008c4a6f2dc4221211b0d7770109a}{yyjson\_mut\_arr\_with\_strn}}(doc,\ vals,\ lens,\ 3);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_free()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_free()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a7a5f504993031f912d06777b8a7b5aff} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Release the JSON document and free the memory. After calling this function, the {\ttfamily doc} and all values from the {\ttfamily doc} are no longer available. This function will do nothing if the {\ttfamily doc} is NULL. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 14
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aa33ac310f363ace5f4dda3697b2c0123}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_get\_root()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aa33ac310f363ace5f4dda3697b2c0123} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+get\+\_\+root (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the root value of this JSON document. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily doc} is NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a797642b2f815a4f05db03ef87f08cc4f}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_imut\_copy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a797642b2f815a4f05db03ef87f08cc4f} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+imut\+\_\+copy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies and returns a new immutable document from input, returns NULL on error. This makes a {\ttfamily deep-\/copy} on the mutable document. The returned document should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily mut\+\_\+doc} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily imut\+\_\+doc}. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a6ee1dc133fa773528286cd0b25300cb2} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+mut\+\_\+copy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies and returns a new mutable document from input, returns NULL on error. This makes a {\ttfamily deep-\/copy} on the mutable document. If allocator is NULL, the default allocator will be used. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily mut\+\_\+doc} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily mut\+\_\+doc}. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\em new\+\_\+val} & The new value to replace the old one. \\
\hline
{\em ctx} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to store the result context, or NULL if not needed. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to store the error information, or NULL if not needed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The old value that was replaced, or NULL if not found. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets the root value of this JSON document. Pass NULL to clear root value of the document. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aec93f33123755af4dfa25c1335a44184}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_str\_pool\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aec93f33123755af4dfa25c1335a44184} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+set\+\_\+str\+\_\+pool\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the string pool size for a mutable document. This function does not allocate memory immediately, but uses the size when the next memory allocation is needed.

If the caller knows the approximate bytes of strings that the document needs to store (e.\+g. copy string with {\ttfamily yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strcpy} function), setting a larger size can avoid multiple memory allocations and improve performance.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & The mutable document. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The desired string pool size in bytes (total string length). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if size is 0 or overflow. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a9dd1f854542f298e963f0912a5a0e002}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size@{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size()}{yyjson\_mut\_doc\_set\_val\_pool\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a9dd1f854542f298e963f0912a5a0e002} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc\+\_\+set\+\_\+val\+\_\+pool\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the value pool size for a mutable document. This function does not allocate memory immediately, but uses the size when the next memory allocation is needed.

If the caller knows the approximate number of values that the document needs to store (e.\+g. create new value with {\ttfamily yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+xxx} functions), setting a larger size can avoid multiple memory allocations and improve performance.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em doc} & The mutable document. \\
\hline
{\em count} & The desired value pool size (number of {\ttfamily \doxylink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}}). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if size is 0 or overflow. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns false if {\ttfamily val} is NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aad64266ebfbdd2a9627050cf1f3f48d7}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch@{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch@{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch()}{yyjson\_mut\_merge\_patch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aad64266ebfbdd2a9627050cf1f3f48d7} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+merge\+\_\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{orig}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{patch}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a merge-\/patched JSON value (RFC 7386). The memory of the returned value is allocated by the {\ttfamily doc}. Returns NULL if the patch could not be applied.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a721dacf0e32ee6c7f18817aca806e9b2} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a mutable object, returns NULL on error. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ac0e1bcd9f449e4b1e62d25fb96830a62}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ac0e1bcd9f449e4b1e62d25fb96830a62} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+add (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a key-\/value pair at the end of the object. This function allows duplicated key in one object. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em obj} & The object to which the new key-\/value pair is to be added. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a string which is created by {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ae8d7e4c75adb1b9adb2246165491a4a3}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+str()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a13c39f37c6936907c266ba9c076dd741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strn()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a95300bcf1cdb52d296e39aa1a4650741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strcpy()}} or {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a1588bdc6f4125e5c6d1daf6b240f6ff8}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strncpy()}}. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The value to add to the object. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Whether successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a1d27c9ad366209b83f236d74ec7e1991}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_arr@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_arr}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_arr()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_arr()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a1d27c9ad366209b83f236d74ec7e1991} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+add\+\_\+arr (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and adds a new array to the target object. The {\ttfamily key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string. This function allows duplicated key in one object.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The key string is not copied, you should keep these strings unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The new array, or NULL on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a996f8aa51f4c1475448974cf98f28df3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+add\+\_\+str (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyWarning}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strcpy()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strcpy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_abeeca08e3b6994dddd55951a83cd648f} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+add\+\_\+strcpy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a string value at the end of the object. The {\ttfamily key} and {\ttfamily val} should be null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 strings. The value string is copied. This function allows duplicated key in one object.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The key string is not copied, you should keep the string unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a4530f9fc02f8604cef3de273feb4ab6a}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_add\_strn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a4530f9fc02f8604cef3de273feb4ab6a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+add\+\_\+strn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a string value at the end of the object. The {\ttfamily key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string. The {\ttfamily val} should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. The {\ttfamily len} should be the length of the {\ttfamily val}, in bytes. This function allows duplicated key in one object.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The key/value strings are not copied, you should keep these strings unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a1d544048860a8c53510d560b4d60411a}

Adds a string value at the end of the object. The {\ttfamily key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string. The {\ttfamily val} should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. The {\ttfamily len} should be the length of the {\ttfamily val}, in bytes. This function allows duplicated key in one object.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The key strings are not copied, you should keep these strings unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

The key string is not copied, you should keep the string unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_get()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a90a824479a3d07f47e9bcce9bbbfcdc0} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value to which the specified key is mapped. Returns NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily obj/key} is NULL, or type is not object.

The {\ttfamily key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a9f40302607516131c026ca5f13a29946}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_getn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_getn}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_getn()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_getn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a9f40302607516131c026ca5f13a29946} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+getn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{key\+\_\+len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value to which the specified key is mapped. Returns NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily obj/key} is NULL, or type is not object.

The {\ttfamily key} should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. The {\ttfamily key\+\_\+len} should be the length of the key, in bytes.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a98e9f97614fce2a6187473eeb35274e8}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_insert@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_insert}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a98e9f97614fce2a6187473eeb35274e8} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{idx}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Inserts a key-\/value pair to the object at the given position. This function allows duplicated key in one object. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em obj} & The object to which the new key-\/value pair is to be added. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a string which is created by {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ae8d7e4c75adb1b9adb2246165491a4a3}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+str()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a13c39f37c6936907c266ba9c076dd741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strn()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a95300bcf1cdb52d296e39aa1a4650741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strcpy()}} or {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a1588bdc6f4125e5c6d1daf6b240f6ff8}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strncpy()}}. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The value to add to the object. \\
\hline
{\em idx} & The index to which to insert the new pair. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Whether successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a9e79f1480256c6e2e8dfbf61da9cd853}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a9e79f1480256c6e2e8dfbf61da9cd853} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__obj__iter}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iter}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Iterates to a specified key and returns the value.

This function does the same thing as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a90a824479a3d07f47e9bcce9bbbfcdc0}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+get()}}, but is much faster if the ordering of the keys is known at compile-\/time and you are using the same order to look up the values. If the key exists in this object, then the iterator will stop at the next key, otherwise the iterator will not change and NULL is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em iter} & The object iterator, should not be NULL. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a UTF-\/8 string with null-\/terminator. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value to which the specified key is mapped. NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key or input is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if the key is not nearby. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aaa4bef14b71ff145fe8cdc2fa98c7f45}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_get\_val()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aaa4bef14b71ff145fe8cdc2fa98c7f45} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+get\+\_\+val (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value for key inside the iteration. If {\ttfamily iter} is NULL, this function will return NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a3d3ab359890ab167041732a871ab943d}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_iter\_getn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a3d3ab359890ab167041732a871ab943d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+getn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__obj__iter}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iter}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{key\+\_\+len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Iterates to a specified key and returns the value.

This function does the same thing as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a9f40302607516131c026ca5f13a29946}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+getn()}} but is much faster if the ordering of the keys is known at compile-\/time and you are using the same order to look up the values. If the key exists in this object, then the iterator will stop at the next key, otherwise the iterator will not change and NULL is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em iter} & The object iterator, should not be NULL. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. \\
\hline
{\em key\+\_\+len} & The the length of {\ttfamily key}, in bytes. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value to which the specified key is mapped. NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key or input is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if the key is not nearby. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_acbfde7c1173b4258f83029c6dacf47c3} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+put (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets a key-\/value pair at the end of the object. This function may remove all key-\/value pairs for the given key before add. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em obj} & The object to which the new key-\/value pair is to be added. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a string which is created by {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_ae8d7e4c75adb1b9adb2246165491a4a3}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+str()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a13c39f37c6936907c266ba9c076dd741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strn()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a95300bcf1cdb52d296e39aa1a4650741}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strcpy()}} or {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a1588bdc6f4125e5c6d1daf6b240f6ff8}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+strncpy()}}. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The value to add to the object. If this value is null, the behavior is same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a660d533ce8b661e85c5b14e4e99e5085}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+remove()}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
Whether successful. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ae6dfd237f7997125e606d678b3b59b5c}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_remove\_strn@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_remove\_strn}}

Removes all key-\/value pairs for the given key. Returns the first value to which the specified key is mapped or NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aea65c64007cfa236faa17e1ac87c4e5e}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_rename\_key@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_rename\_key}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aea65c64007cfa236faa17e1ac87c4e5e} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+obj\+\_\+rename\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{new\+\_\+key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Replaces all matching keys with the new key. Returns true if at least one key was renamed. The {\ttfamily key} and {\ttfamily new\+\_\+key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string. The {\ttfamily new\+\_\+key} is copied and held by doc.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time. If {\ttfamily new\+\_\+key} already exists, it will cause duplicate keys. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a0f1a9fea8fbc13caf61861dfdb498d46}

Rotates key-\/value pairs in the object for the given number of times. For example\+: {\ttfamily \{"{}a"{}\+:1,"{}b"{}\+:2,"{}c"{}\+:3,"{}d"{}\+:4\}} rotate 1 is {\ttfamily \{"{}b"{}\+:2,"{}c"{}\+:3,"{}d"{}\+:4,"{}a"{}\+:1\}}.

\end{DoxyReturn}

This function takes a linear search time. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Returns the number of key-\/value pairs in this object. Returns 0 if {\ttfamily obj} is NULL or type is not object. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_afc2749d9ed694b6d0a4f5c14da19c7d4}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_kv@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_kv}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_kv()}{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_kv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_afc2749d9ed694b6d0a4f5c14da19c7d4}

Creates and returns a mutable object with key-\/value pairs and pair count, returns NULL on error. The keys and values are not copied. The strings should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The input string is not copied, you should keep this string unmodified for the lifetime of this JSON document.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a49cfc79051b729689f4f08592b284cc9}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_str@{yyjson\_mut\_obj\_with\_str}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a49cfc79051b729689f4f08592b284cc9}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_patch()}{yyjson\_mut\_patch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ad4cca957150bd6f19fa12a4f907dffee} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{orig}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{patch}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__patch__err}{yyjson\+\_\+patch\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and returns a patched JSON value (RFC 6902). The memory of the returned value is allocated by the {\ttfamily doc}. The {\ttfamily err} is used to receive error information, pass NULL if not needed. Returns NULL if the patch could not be applied. 函数调用图\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ab49d3e532c97846b198b360602a9b5ca} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+ptr\+\_\+add (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{new\+\_\+val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add (insert) value by a JSON pointer. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The target JSON value. \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & The JSON pointer string (UTF-\/8 with null-\/terminator). \\
\hline
{\em doc} & Only used to create new values when needed. \\
\hline
{\em new\+\_\+val} & The value to be added. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if JSON pointer is valid and new value is added, false otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The parent nodes will be created if they do not exist. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a4de077663ebedc11a24ddbde66a72945}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set@{yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set@{yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set()}{yyjson\_mut\_ptr\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a4de077663ebedc11a24ddbde66a72945} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+ptr\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{new\+\_\+val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set value by a JSON pointer. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The target JSON value. \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & The JSON pointer string (UTF-\/8 with null-\/terminator). \\
\hline
{\em new\+\_\+val} & The value to be set, pass NULL to remove. \\
\hline
{\em doc} & Only used to create new values when needed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if JSON pointer is valid and new value is set, false otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The parent nodes will be created if they do not exist. If the target value already exists, it will be replaced by the new value. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ac8ba98e62d5d4c5ab9ddd44173164756} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+ptr\+\_\+setn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ptr}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{new\+\_\+val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set value by a JSON pointer. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The target JSON value. \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & The JSON pointer string (UTF-\/8, null-\/terminator is not required). \\
\hline
{\em len} & The length of {\ttfamily ptr} in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em new\+\_\+val} & The value to be set, pass NULL to remove. \\
\hline
{\em doc} & Only used to create new values when needed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if JSON pointer is valid and new value is set, false otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The parent nodes will be created if they do not exist. If the target value already exists, it will be replaced by the new value. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{yyjson\_mut\_read\_number@{yyjson\_mut\_read\_number}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_read\_number()}{yyjson\_mut\_read\_number()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aed1fdeb679986591d5f2f257c5cf3b60} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+read\+\_\+number (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read a JSON number.

This function is thread-\/safe when data is not modified by other threads.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The output value where result is stored. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. The value will hold either \doxylink{test__malloc__compliance_8cpp_a36cb3b01d81ffd844bbbfb54003e06ec}{UINT} or SINT or \doxylink{fft_8h_a5821460e95a0800cf9f24c38915cbbde}{REAL} number; \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. Supports {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+NUMBER\+\_\+\+AS\+\_\+\+RAW} and {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+INF\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+NAN}. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used for long number. It is only used when the built-\/in floating point reader is disabled. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
If successful, a pointer to the character after the last character used in the conversion, NULL if an error occurs. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a7a142af553e7831989593aee44f74e26} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val\+\_\+imut\+\_\+copy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies and returns a new immutable document from input, returns NULL on error. This makes a {\ttfamily deep-\/copy} on the mutable value. The returned document should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily mut\+\_\+val} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily imut\+\_\+doc}. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function is recursive and may cause a stack overflow if the object level is too deep. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a700da5ce5bf8bb9d3739cc73a0f51cdf}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_val\_write@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write()}{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a700da5ce5bf8bb9d3739cc73a0f51cdf} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val\+\_\+write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON string.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+: The {\ttfamily val} is not modified by other threads.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em len} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive output length in bytes (not including the null-\/terminator). Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need length information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 22
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_adf8b2d3c8b57e85d58108d58c68b0db5}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_mut\_val\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_adf8b2d3c8b57e85d58108d58c68b0db5} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__val}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily val} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The mutable JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 23

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The mutable JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em len} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive output length in bytes (not including the null-\/terminator). Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need length information. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()} or alc-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ad2a7aa77fa66a593536e3d7c3edb1d7a}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_mut\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file}}
\index{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file@{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_mut\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ad2a7aa77fa66a593536e3d7c3edb1d7a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__mut__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+mut\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{doc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a document to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily doc} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em doc} & The mutable JSON document. If this doc is NULL or has no root, the function will fail and return false. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a1e8a4dea2e9e9248acde14c664ab702b}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_get@{yyjson\_obj\_get}}
\index{yyjson\_obj\_get@{yyjson\_obj\_get}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_get()}{yyjson\_obj\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a1e8a4dea2e9e9248acde14c664ab702b} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value to which the specified key is mapped. Returns NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily obj/key} is NULL, or type is not object.

The {\ttfamily key} should be a null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a2936ca2492ae8cdcdf0435f5259ff854}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_getn@{yyjson\_obj\_getn}}
\index{yyjson\_obj\_getn@{yyjson\_obj\_getn}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_getn()}{yyjson\_obj\_getn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a2936ca2492ae8cdcdf0435f5259ff854} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+getn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{obj}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{key\+\_\+len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value to which the specified key is mapped. Returns NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key. Returns NULL if {\ttfamily obj/key} is NULL, or type is not object.

The {\ttfamily key} should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. The {\ttfamily key\+\_\+len} should be the length of the key, in bytes.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a1f3b09c4f279287f8af93b3754a41e85}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get}}
\index{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get()}{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a1f3b09c4f279287f8af93b3754a41e85} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__obj__iter}{yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iter}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Iterates to a specified key and returns the value.

This function does the same thing as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a1e8a4dea2e9e9248acde14c664ab702b}{yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+get()}}, but is much faster if the ordering of the keys is known at compile-\/time and you are using the same order to look up the values. If the key exists in this object, then the iterator will stop at the next key, otherwise the iterator will not change and NULL is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em iter} & The object iterator, should not be NULL. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a UTF-\/8 string with null-\/terminator. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value to which the specified key is mapped. NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key or input is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if the key is not nearby. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a3403b9c25c8b8f2b3027f4e6d97d0ca8}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val}}
\index{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val()}{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_get\_val()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a3403b9c25c8b8f2b3027f4e6d97d0ca8} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+get\+\_\+val (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value for key inside the iteration. If {\ttfamily iter} is NULL, this function will return NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a7a45a4b5a1340bb3c2907b7faf3981be}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn}}
\index{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn()}{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_getn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a7a45a4b5a1340bb3c2907b7faf3981be} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+getn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__obj__iter}{yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{iter}{, }\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{key}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{key\+\_\+len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Iterates to a specified key and returns the value.

This function does the same thing as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a2936ca2492ae8cdcdf0435f5259ff854}{yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+getn()}}, but is much faster if the ordering of the keys is known at compile-\/time and you are using the same order to look up the values. If the key exists in this object, then the iterator will stop at the next key, otherwise the iterator will not change and NULL is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em iter} & The object iterator, should not be NULL. \\
\hline
{\em key} & The key, should be a UTF-\/8 string, null-\/terminator is not required. \\
\hline
{\em key\+\_\+len} & The the length of {\ttfamily key}, in bytes. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value to which the specified key is mapped. NULL if this object contains no mapping for the key or input is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
This function takes a linear search time if the key is not nearby. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Returns the next key in the iteration, or NULL on end. If {\ttfamily iter} is NULL, this function will return NULL. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a543806a566821ccc6c7069edabc59a85}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_obj\_iter\_with@{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_with}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_with()}{yyjson\_obj\_iter\_with()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a543806a566821ccc6c7069edabc59a85}

Create an iterator with an object, same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_a2b6a426ece4ffeb9dede1f7a9970140d}{yyjson\+\_\+obj\+\_\+iter\+\_\+init()}}.

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
The iterator does not need to be destroyed. 
\end{DoxyNote}
