\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aeab3c2a1d86225e5b181fb1bba7587d4}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_read@{yyjson\_read}}
\index{yyjson\_read@{yyjson\_read}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read()}{yyjson\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aeab3c2a1d86225e5b181fb1bba7587d4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read a JSON string.

This function is thread-\/safe.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is not required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The length of JSON data in bytes. If this parameter is 0, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON document, or NULL if an error occurs. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a605ac08b083fb65331d7fa5eb5d32225}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_read\_file@{yyjson\_read\_file}}
\index{yyjson\_read\_file@{yyjson\_read\_file}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read\_file()}{yyjson\_read\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a605ac08b083fb65331d7fa5eb5d32225} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read a JSON file.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON reader. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON document, or NULL if an error occurs. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to read. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:

Read JSON from a file pointer.

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ae511cac592355c2f60f170402b9d8dbf}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage@{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage}}
\index{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage@{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage()}{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ae511cac592355c2f60f170402b9d8dbf} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} size\+\_\+t yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+max\+\_\+memory\+\_\+usage (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the size of maximum memory usage to read a JSON data.

You may use this value to avoid \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a99aa8fd9f4831e1b0fa9e1cdcde3e249}{malloc()} or \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a84e191d73dd91ea0a5bd2ec14d7adfaf}{calloc()} call inside the reader to get better performance, or read multiple JSON with one piece of memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em len} & The length of JSON data in bytes. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The maximum memory size to read this JSON, or 0 if overflow.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Example}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ read\ multiple\ JSON\ with\ same\ pre-\/allocated\ memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ *dat1,\ *dat2,\ *dat3;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ JSON\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ len1,\ len2,\ len3;\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ JSON\ length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ max\_len\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{runtime_2xx_hash_2tests_2collisions_2main_8c_afa99ec4acc4ecb2dc3c2d05da15d0e3f}{MAX}}(len1,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{runtime_2xx_hash_2tests_2collisions_2main_8c_afa99ec4acc4ecb2dc3c2d05da15d0e3f}{MAX}}(len2,\ len3));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\_doc}}\ *doc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ use\ one\ allocator\ for\ multiple\ JSON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{size}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_ae511cac592355c2f60f170402b9d8dbf}{yyjson\_read\_max\_memory\_usage}}(max\_len,\ 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ *buf\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc-override_8h_a99aa8fd9f4831e1b0fa9e1cdcde3e249}{malloc}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{size}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\_alc}}\ alc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a6068c4293a2b35493b18421b9afbd3d5}{yyjson\_alc\_pool\_init}}(\&alc,\ buf,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{size}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ no\ more\ alloc()\ or\ realloc()\ call\ during\ reading}}
\DoxyCodeLine{doc\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}{yyjson\_read\_opts}}(dat1,\ len1,\ 0,\ \&alc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\_doc\_free}}(doc);}
\DoxyCodeLine{doc\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}{yyjson\_read\_opts}}(dat2,\ len2,\ 0,\ \&alc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\_doc\_free}}(doc);}
\DoxyCodeLine{doc\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}{yyjson\_read\_opts}}(dat3,\ len3,\ 0,\ \&alc,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\_doc\_free}}(doc);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free}}(buf);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a2b7dfa8495fb1d839e6294f2e7c4b58a}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_read\_number@{yyjson\_read\_number}}
\index{yyjson\_read\_number@{yyjson\_read\_number}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read\_number()}{yyjson\_read\_number()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a2b7dfa8495fb1d839e6294f2e7c4b58a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+number (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read a JSON number.

This function is thread-\/safe when data is not modified by other threads.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The output value where result is stored. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. The value will hold either \doxylink{test__malloc__compliance_8cpp_a36cb3b01d81ffd844bbbfb54003e06ec}{UINT} or SINT or \doxylink{fft_8h_a5821460e95a0800cf9f24c38915cbbde}{REAL} number; \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. Supports {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+NUMBER\+\_\+\+AS\+\_\+\+RAW} and {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+INF\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+NAN}. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used for long number. It is only used when the built-\/in floating point reader is disabled. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
If successful, a pointer to the character after the last character used in the conversion, NULL if an error occurs. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_read\_opts@{yyjson\_read\_opts}}
\index{yyjson\_read\_opts@{yyjson\_read\_opts}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_read\_opts()}{yyjson\_read\_opts()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_acf234d21f0cb4b7fc89381ef25e9f0a8} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__doc}{yyjson\+\_\+doc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+opts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dat}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{len}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__read__err}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Read JSON with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The {\ttfamily dat} is not modified by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em dat} & The JSON data (UTF-\/8 without BOM), null-\/terminator is not required. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. The {\ttfamily dat} will not be modified without the flag {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+INSITU}, so you can pass a {\ttfamily const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} string and case it to {\ttfamily char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} if you don\textquotesingle{}t use the {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+INSITU} flag. \\
\hline
{\em len} & The length of JSON data in bytes. If this parameter is 0, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON read options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON reader. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON document, or NULL if an error occurs. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{yyjson_8h_adad98bd766cf52d99f2c54dcb120786d}{yyjson\+\_\+doc\+\_\+free()}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a00409eb59aee687f7778d00510b59d38}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_val\_write@{yyjson\_val\_write}}
\index{yyjson\_val\_write@{yyjson\_val\_write}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_val\_write()}{yyjson\_val\_write()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a00409eb59aee687f7778d00510b59d38} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a682886dc8be2307076b125b496b15570}{yyjson\+\_\+api\+\_\+inline}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} yyjson\+\_\+val\+\_\+write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{len}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON string.

This function is thread-\/safe.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em val} & The JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em len} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive output length in bytes (not including the null-\/terminator). Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need length information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 37
\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a725cc27bd7bd37c1d18c41589abd34db}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!yyjson\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_val\_write\_file}}
\index{yyjson\_val\_write\_file@{yyjson\_val\_write\_file}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yyjson\_val\_write\_file()}{yyjson\_val\_write\_file()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a725cc27bd7bd37c1d18c41589abd34db} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a691136e772913e98860a791e65b70f04}{yyjson\+\_\+api}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} yyjson\+\_\+val\+\_\+write\+\_\+file (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{path}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__val}{yyjson\+\_\+val}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}}}]{flg}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__alc}{yyjson\+\_\+alc}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{alc}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structyyjson__write__err}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+err}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{err}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write a value to JSON file with options.

This function is thread-\/safe when\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The file is not accessed by other threads.
\item The {\ttfamily alc} is thread-\/safe or NULL.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em path} & The JSON file\textquotesingle{}s path. If this path is NULL or invalid, the function will fail and return false. If this file is not empty, the content will be discarded. \\
\hline
{\em val} & The JSON root value. If this parameter is NULL, the function will fail and return NULL. \\
\hline
{\em flg} & The JSON write options. Multiple options can be combined with {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} operator. 0 means no options. \\
\hline
{\em alc} & The memory allocator used by JSON writer. Pass NULL to use the libc\textquotesingle{}s default allocator. \\
\hline
{\em err} & \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} pointer to receive error information. Pass NULL if you don\textquotesingle{}t need error information. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if successful, false if an error occurs.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
On 32-\/bit operating system, files larger than 2GB may fail to write. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
函数调用图\+:
% FIG 38

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} new JSON string, or NULL if an error occurs. This string is encoded as UTF-\/8 with a null-\/terminator. When it\textquotesingle{}s no longer needed, it should be freed with \doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()} or alc-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{mimalloc-override_8h_a9d4b5df3530d1bc733070a4669ba6ebc}{free()}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Allow inf/nan number and literal, case-\/insensitive, such as 1e999, NaN, inf, -\/Infinity (non-\/standard). \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_abdbf139ee03d263c8a833fbef8cbf63c}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE@{YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE}}
\index{YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE@{YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE}{YYJSON\_READ\_ALLOW\_INVALID\_UNICODE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_abdbf139ee03d263c8a833fbef8cbf63c} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}} YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+INVALID\+\_\+\+UNICODE = 1 $<$$<$ 6\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Allow reading invalid unicode when parsing string values (non-\/standard). Invalid characters will be allowed to appear in the string values, but invalid escape sequences will still be reported as errors. This flag does not affect the performance of correctly encoded strings.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Strings in JSON values may contain incorrect encoding when this option is used, you need to handle these strings carefully to avoid security risks. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Unexpected ending, such as {\ttfamily \mbox{[}123}. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aa476cdc60442393b93dd0474ed4f08bc}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU@{YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU}}
\index{YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU@{YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU}{YYJSON\_READ\_INSITU}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_aa476cdc60442393b93dd0474ed4f08bc} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}} YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+INSITU = 1 $<$$<$ 0\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Read the input data in-\/situ. This option allows the reader to modify and use input data to store string values, which can increase reading speed slightly. The caller should hold the input data before free the document. The input data must be padded by at least {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+PADDING\+\_\+\+SIZE} bytes. For example\+: {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]}} should be {\ttfamily \mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]}\textbackslash{}0\textbackslash{}0\textbackslash{}0\textbackslash{}0}, input length should be 5. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a8940a4ae4ba3467bb7bc6c5ee3deb2ea}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG@{YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG}}
\index{YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG@{YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG}{YYJSON\_READ\_NOFLAG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a8940a4ae4ba3467bb7bc6c5ee3deb2ea} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}} YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+NOFLAG = 0\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Default option (RFC 8259 compliant)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Read positive integer as \doxylink{eabase_8h_aaa5d1cd013383c889537491c3cfd9aad}{uint64\+\_\+t}.
\item Read negative integer as \doxylink{eabase_8h_adec1df1b8b51cb32b77e5b86fff46471}{int64\+\_\+t}.
\item Read floating-\/point number as double with round-\/to-\/nearest mode.
\item Read integer which cannot fit in \doxylink{eabase_8h_aaa5d1cd013383c889537491c3cfd9aad}{uint64\+\_\+t} or \doxylink{eabase_8h_adec1df1b8b51cb32b77e5b86fff46471}{int64\+\_\+t} as double.
\item Report error if double number is infinity.
\item Report error if string contains invalid UTF-\/8 character or BOM.
\item Report error on trailing commas, comments, inf and nan literals. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a1cafb3655e6e9e60f019d2b7a9bf79c2}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW@{YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW}}
\index{YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW@{YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW}!yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW}{YYJSON\_READ\_NUMBER\_AS\_RAW}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_a1cafb3655e6e9e60f019d2b7a9bf79c2} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a36af676813028c1360e8b343768f0e81}{yyjson\+\_\+read\+\_\+flag}} YYJSON\+\_\+\+READ\+\_\+\+NUMBER\+\_\+\+AS\+\_\+\+RAW = 1 $<$$<$ 5\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Read all numbers as raw strings (value with {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+RAW} type), inf/nan literal is also read as raw with {\ttfamily ALLOW\+\_\+\+INF\+\_\+\+AND\+\_\+\+NAN} flag. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ad2fb99734b237a7af74924443fe5260e}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_STOP\_WHEN\_DONE@{YYJSON\_READ\_STOP\_WHEN\_DONE}}

Stop when done instead of issuing an error if there\textquotesingle{}s additional content after a JSON document. This option may be used to parse small pieces of JSON in larger data, such as {\ttfamily NDJSON}. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a5b8948d47748a81d6a4abf94949e0e88}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_READ\_SUCCESS@{YYJSON\_READ\_SUCCESS}}

Allow invalid unicode when encoding string values (non-\/standard). Invalid characters in string value will be copied byte by byte. If {\ttfamily YYJSON\+\_\+\+WRITE\+\_\+\+ESCAPE\+\_\+\+UNICODE} flag is also set, invalid character will be escaped as {\ttfamily U+\+FFFD} (replacement character). This flag does not affect the performance of correctly encoded strings. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_a41cb8e304e08d7455f43c753bfa19b82}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_WRITE\_ERROR\_FILE\_OPEN@{YYJSON\_WRITE\_ERROR\_FILE\_OPEN}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ab0cfae40d7ae6489d73c6cf5db9c09e1}

Adds a newline character {\ttfamily \textbackslash{}n} at the end of the JSON. This can be helpful for text editors or NDJSON. \Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_ae152a6e8e8c6e4efd798fa6eca9d311f}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_WRITE\_NOFLAG@{YYJSON\_WRITE\_NOFLAG}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{YYJSON\_WRITE\_NOFLAG}{YYJSON\_WRITE\_NOFLAG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{yyjson_8h_ae152a6e8e8c6e4efd798fa6eca9d311f} 
const \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_afb7989387fc481f678e13325c18e6338}{yyjson\+\_\+write\+\_\+flag}} YYJSON\+\_\+\+WRITE\+\_\+\+NOFLAG = 0\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Default option\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Write JSON minify.
\item Report error on inf or nan number.
\item Report error on invalid UTF-\/8 string.
\item Do not escape unicode or slash. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{yyjson_8h_aebdaa55a1673e99d2dcea01a15c633be}\index{yyjson.h@{yyjson.h}!YYJSON\_WRITE\_PRETTY@{YYJSON\_WRITE\_PRETTY}}
